<script>
            require([
                "jquery",
            ], function ($) {
                "use strict";
                $(".input_filter_barcode").keyup(function() {
                 readBarcode(event, this)
                });
                $(".reset_barcode").click(function() {
                   resetBarcode();
                });
                function readBarcode(event, ele){
                    var value = $(ele).val();
                    if(value) {
                        var key = event.which || event.keyCode;
                        if(key == Event.KEY_RETURN){
                            production_request_to_stock_gridJsObject.doFilterValues({
                                    barcode: value+ ",barcodeorder"
                                })
                            production_request_to_stock_gridJsObject.doFilter();
                            $( document ).ajaxStop(function() {
                                production_request_to_stock_grid_massactionJsObject.selectAll();
                            });
                        }
                    }
                }

                function resetBarcode() {
                    production_request_to_stock_gridJsObject.doFilterValues({
                             barcode: "0ZZ4ADX!000"
                    })
                    $( document ).ajaxStop(function() {
                        production_request_to_stock_grid_massactionJsObject.unselectAll();
                    });
                }
                var columnActionToTop =  $(".admin__data-grid-wrap.admin__data-grid-wrap-static")[0].offsetTop;
                var customFilterDivHeight = $(".admin__data-grid-header-bottom")[0].offsetTop;
                var multiSelectHeight = $(".action-select-multiselect").height() * 0.75;
                var marginTop = columnActionToTop - customFilterDivHeight + multiSelectHeight;
                $(".mass-select-wrap").css("margin-top",marginTop);
            });

    require(['jquery', 'underscore'], function ($, _) {
        function attach() {
            var $cronExpressions = $('input.cron-expression, .cron-expression input[type="text"]');

            if ($cronExpressions.length) {
                require(['Mirasvit_Core/js/utils/cron-expression'], function (cron) {
                    $cronExpressions.each(function (key, el) {
                        cron(el);
                    })
                });
            }

            var $regularExpressions = $('input.regular-expression');

            if ($regularExpressions.length) {
                require(['Mirasvit_Core/js/utils/regular-expression'], function (regular) {
                    $regularExpressions.each(function (key, el) {
                        regular(el);
                    })
                });
            }
        }

        attach();

        var throttledAttach = _.throttle(attach, 100);

        var observer = new MutationObserver(throttledAttach);

        observer.observe(document.body, {
            subtree:   true,
            childList: true
        });
    })
